beginSubroutine: s32'cosShotCheck'
  ifPlayerCharacter: s16'cos'
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(1)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg1), Val(0)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
          runOnObject: (PLAYER)
            storeValue: Mem(CPUVal7), Val(1)
          endRunOnObject: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      else: 
        runOnObject: (PLAYER)
          storeValue: Mem(CPUVal7), Val(1)
        endRunOnObject: 
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      runOnObject: (PLAYER)
        storeValue: Mem(CPUVal7), Val(0)
      endRunOnObject: 
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginState: s32'cmn_TrialTokeiMain'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    linkObjPosition: 3
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Mem(SentToObject0)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Mem(SentToObject1)
    ifPlayerCharacter: s16'cos'
      runOnObject: (PLAYER)
        storeValue: Mem(CPUVal7), Val(0)
      endRunOnObject: 
    endIf: 
    upon: (SIGNAL0)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
      if: Mem(ActReg0)
        callPrivateFunction: s32'TrialReadyGo', 0, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0
      endIf: 
      else: 
        if: Mem(ActReg1)
        endIf: 
        callPrivateFunction: s32'TrialReadyGo', 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0
        deactivateObjectByName: s32'cmn_TrialTokeiMain'
      endElse: 
    endUpon: 
    upon: (IDLING)
      callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cosShotCheck', Val(1), Val(1), Val(0), Val(0)
      if: Mem(ActReg2)
        if: Mem(ActReg0)
          if: Mem(TrialReadyGo)
            if: Mem(ActReg1)
            endIf: 
            deactivateObjectByName: s32'cmn_TrialTokeiMain'
            callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cosShotCheck', Val(0), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'null', 2147483647
endState: 

beginState: s32'cmn_MissionCtrl'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)

    missionSealAttack: 1

      missionSealFDash: 0
    endIf: 
    upon: (IDLING)
      isObjectActive: (STACK0)

      endIf: 
      else:

          modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
          ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(180)
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endElse: 
    endUpon:

      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
    upon: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK_AFTER_FIX_PARAM)
      missionMiss: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'null', 2147483647
endState:

    upon: (ENEMY_GUARD_AFTER_FIX_PARAM)
      missionMiss: 
    endUpon: 
    upon: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK_AFTER_FIX_PARAM)
      missionMiss: 
    endUpon: 
    upon: (PLAYER_GUARD_AFTER_FIX_PARAM)
      missionMiss: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon:

endState:

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnEntryToStand2P'
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Mem(FuncArg0)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Mem(FuncArg1)
  upon: (IDLING)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(0)
      displayModel: 0
      lockScreenPosition: 1
      checkScreenCollision: 0
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(1)
      callSubroutine: s32'cmnEntryToStandEx'
      setPositionXInBattle: -402000
      warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(-252000), Val(0), Mem(ActReg1)
      modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Val(-2500), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(PosZ)
      setDepthSpeed: 0, 2500
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Mem(ActReg0)
      displayModel: 1
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Mem(ActReg1)
      lockScreenPosition: 0
      checkScreenCollision: 1
      physicsXImpulse: 0, 0
      setDepthSpeed: 0, 0
      setPositionXInBattle: -252000
      setDepth: 0
      haltMomentum: 1
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnEntryToStandEx'
  storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ActReg2), (ENEMY), Mem(ActReg0)
  storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ActReg3), (ENEMY), Mem(ActReg1)
  ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(0)
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActReg2)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(0)
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg3)
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnactmatchwin'
  calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_X_FRONT), (PLAYER), (PLAYER), (To3_ENEMY_MAIN_PLAYER), (PLAYER)
  storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaActReg6), Mem(Tmp)
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(CmnCharaActReg6), Val(0)
    flipDirection: 
  endIf: 
  setEventTrigger: (TIMER), 1
  upon: (TIMER)
    setNoCollision: 1
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnactroundwin'
  setEventTrigger: (TIMER), 2
  upon: (TIMER)
    setNoCollision: 1
    pushboxCollisionSameSide: 1
    ifNot: Mem(IsMainPlayerSelf)
      checkCurrentStateName: (To3_MAIN_PLAYER), s32'CmnActMatchWin'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        jumpToState: s32'AssistResult'
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(2)
        setPushboxWidth: 150000
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(3)
        setPushboxWidth: 160000
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(4)
        setPushboxWidth: 170000
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(5)
        setPushboxWidth: 180000
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(6)
        setPushboxWidth: 190000
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(7)
        setPushboxWidth: 200000
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine:

          storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg10), Val(1)
        endIf: 
        else: 
          storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg10), Val(2)
        endElse:

    endIf:

    if: Mem(Tmp)

      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg8), Val(4)

        endIf:

        endElse: 
      endIf:

      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg8), Val(2)
      endIf: 
    endIf:

    if: Mem(Tmp)
      checkInput: (INPUT_8_ELM_TRG)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg8), Val(8)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    checkInput: (INPUT_DASH_STRICT)
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg8), Val(6)
      checkInput: (INPUT_6)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg8), Val(6)
        ifNot: Mem(CtrlDir)
          storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg10), Val(1)
        endIf: 
        else: 
          storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg10), Val(2)
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      checkInput: (INPUT_4)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg8), Val(4)
        ifNot: Mem(CtrlDir)
          storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg10), Val(1)
        endIf: 
        else: 
          storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg10), Val(2)
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      checkInput: (INPUT_2)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg8), Val(2)
      endIf: 
      checkInput: (INPUT_8)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg8), Val(8)
      endIf: 
      checkInput: (INPUT_1)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg8), Val(0)
      endIf: 
      checkInput: (INPUT_3)
      if: Mem(Tmp)

      endIf:

      endIf:

      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg8), Val(0)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    if: Mem(CmnCharaReg8)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(CmnCharaReg8), Val(100)
        modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(CmnCharaReg8), Val(100)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(CmnCharaReg8), Val(10)
      endIf: 
      ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(CmnCharaReg8), Val(-1)

          storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg8), Val(0)
          storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg10), Val(0)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
    if: Mem(CmnCharaReg6)

        addTension: 1
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(TensionBalance), Val(25000)
        addTensionBalance: 0, 50
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(CmnCharaReg9)
    if: Mem(IsLand)
      storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg9), Val(0)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  isObjectActive: (STACK_CMN_ACT)
  ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
    createObject: s32'cmnWSBDummy', (PLAYER)
    stackObject: (STACK_CMN_ACT), (PREVIOUS)
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'cmn_wall_dir'
  if: Mem(CmnCharaReg7)
    upon: (WALL)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (WALL)
      fadeOutStart: 1000, 0
      pushboxFix: 1
      checkMoveFlag: (CLOSE_TO_LEFT_CORNER)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        faceRight: 
      endIf: 
      checkMoveFlag: (CLOSE_TO_RIGHT_CORNER)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        faceLeft: 
      endIf: 
      screenAdditionalWidth: -10000
      addPositionX: 0, -10000
      addPositionY: 0, 1
      ignorePushback: 1
      wallTouchTime: 
      invulnForce: 1
      runOnObject: (ENEMY)
        invulnForce: 1
      endRunOnObject: 
      upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(2)
          ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(CheckStop), Val(3)
            clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
            invulnForce: 0
            runOnObject: (ENEMY)
              invulnForce: 0
            endRunOnObject: 
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(2)
            clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
            invulnForce: 0
            runOnObject: (ENEMY)
              invulnForce: 0
            endRunOnObject: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endUpon: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'cmn_AtkLv0'
  if: Mem(IsPlayer)
    initializeAttackCategoryByCurrent: 
  endIf: 
  attackLevel: 0
  hitstunAmount: 12
  blockstunAmount: 9
  riscGain: 5
  ifNot: Mem(IsPlayer)
    riscGain: 5
    attackReflect: 1
    attackFrontDirection: (SELF)
    attackIgnoreCaution: 1
  endIf: 
  riscConsume: 10
  prorationTandan: 0
  hitStop: 11
  ifNot: Mem(FuncArg3)
    tensionGainOnConnect: 30
  endIf: 
  else: 
    tensionGainOnConnect: 15
  endIf: 
  preGuardRange: Val(190)
  preGuardRangeY: 0, 250
  rollCount: 1
  if: Mem(IsLand)
    hitAirPushbackX: Val(21500)
    hitAirPushbackY: Val(30000)
    hitGravity: Val(3000)
  endIf: 
  else: 
    hitAirPushbackX: Val(21500)
    hitAirPushbackY: Val(10000)
    hitGravity: Val(3500)
  endElse: 
  forcedComboScaleCount: 5
  considerHitAirPushbackX: 15
  considerHitAirPushbackY: 15
  airGuardPushbackX: 0
  faultlessDefenseMinimumPushback: 75
  guardCrushPushback: 50
  if: Mem(IsPlayer)
    wallPushback: 250
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(IsPlayer)
    guardLandingAction: 1
    airBlockstunAddition: 15
  endIf: 
  attackPositiveBonus: 1
  upon: (COUNTER_HIT)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (COUNTER_HIT)
    if: Mem(IsPlayer)
      callSubroutine: s32'cmn_RISCounter'
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmnAtk_GB_TGG', Mem(FuncArg0), Mem(FuncArg1), Val(1), Mem(FuncArg3)
  if: Mem(IsPlayer)
    callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmn_SameAttack', Val(2), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
  endIf: 
  else: 
    callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmn_SameAttack', Val(1), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
  endElse: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'cmn_WSBPoint_Add_Lv0'
  wallDamage: 0
  ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg13)
    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg13), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Val(0), Mem(CmnCharaReg13), Mem(CmnCharaActReg6)
  attackExHitParam: Mem(CmnCharaActReg6), 0, 10000, 1, (ENEMY), Mem(WSBPoint)
  ifOperationInObject: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), (ENEMY), Mem(PosXRaw), Val(750000)
    ifOperationInObject: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), (ENEMY), Mem(PosXRaw), Val(-750000)
      ifOperationInObject: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), (ENEMY), Mem(WSBPoint), Val(1750)
        attackExHitParam: Mem(CmnCharaActReg6), 0, 1500, 1, (ENEMY), Mem(WSBPoint)
        disableWallBreak: 1
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(AdjustmentForScript0)
    debugLogForScript: s32'WSB_Add_Lv0', 0, 0
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

    modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(CmnCharaReg11), Val(10000000), Mem(CmnCharaReg12)
    ifOperation: (MOD), Mem(CmnCharaReg12), Val(2)
      initialComboScaleCount: 0, 5

      initialComboScaleCount: 0, 5

    ifOperation: (MOD), Mem(CmnCharaReg12), Val(2)
      initialComboScaleCount: 0, 5
    endIf:

    ifOperation: (MOD), Mem(CmnCharaReg12), Val(2)
      initialComboScaleCount: 0, 5

    ifOperation: (MOD), Mem(CmnCharaReg12), Val(2)
      initialComboScaleCount: 0, 5

      initialComboScaleCount: 0, 0

      initialComboScaleCount: 0, 0

      initialComboScaleCount: 0, 0

    ifOperation: (MOD), Mem(CmnCharaReg12), Val(2)
      initialComboScaleCount: 0, 20

      runOnObject: (ENEMY)
        slowMoveRate: 0, 0
      endRunOnObject: 
    endIf:

  ifOperationInObject: (IS_LESSER), (PLAYER), Mem(SpeedY), Val(0)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(PosY), Val(150000)
      runOnObject: (PLAYER)
        slowMoveRate: 0, 0

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnCamCounterTrack'
  runOnObject: (STACK0)
    setPosXBetweenObject: 3, 22
    setPosYBetweenObject: 3, 22
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(-1300000)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg6), Val(1300000)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnThrowPosition_Limit'
  endRunOnObject: 
  setPosXBetweenObject: 3, 22
  setPosYBetweenObject: 3, 22
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(PosY), Val(90000)
    storeValue: Mem(PosY), Val(90000)
  endIf: 
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(-1300000)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg6), Val(1300000)
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnThrowPosition_Limit'
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Val(16), Mem(ObjReg2)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(EnemyDistanceY), Val(9), Mem(ObjReg3)
  modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(30)
  modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg3), Val(20)
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(0)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(-1)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg3), Val(0)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg3), Val(-1)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(ObjReg2), Mem(ObjReg3)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Mem(ObjReg2)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(ObjReg3), Val(480000)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Val(480000)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ObjReg3), Val(380000)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Val(380000)
  endIf: 
  storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(130000)
  storeValue: Mem(ObjReg5), Val(130000)
  ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(1)
    ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (ENEMY), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(2)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(70000)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg5), Val(92000)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(100000)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg5), Val(120000)
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(2)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(125000)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg5), Val(125000)
  endIf: 
  storeValue: Mem(ObjReg2), Mem(ObjReg3)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Val(460000), Mem(ObjReg2), Mem(ObjReg2)
  modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(7)
  modifyVar: (DIV), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(-30)
  modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg4), Mem(ObjReg2)
  modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg5), Mem(ObjReg2)
  ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(IsAir), Val(1)
    ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (ENEMY), Mem(IsAir), Val(1)
      storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ObjReg6), (ENEMY), Mem(SpeedY)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(0)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(-4), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg4), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(1), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVar: (DIV), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(6)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg5), Mem(ObjReg7)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(-16), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg4), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(1), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVar: (DIV), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(1)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg5), Mem(ObjReg7)
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(5000)
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ObjReg6), (ENEMY), Mem(DmgAtkAngle)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(0)
        modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(5000)
        modifyVar: (DIV), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(90)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(70), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ObjReg4), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(3), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg5), Mem(ObjReg7)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(5000)
        modifyVar: (DIV), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(90)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(3), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ObjReg4), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(3), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg5), Mem(ObjReg7)
      endElse: 
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ObjReg6), (ENEMY), Mem(DmgAtkAngle)
    ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (ENEMY), Mem(IsLand), Val(1)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(0)
        modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(5000)
        modifyVar: (DIV), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(90)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(40), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ObjReg4), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(2), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg5), Mem(ObjReg7)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(5000)
        modifyVar: (DIV), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(90)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(3), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ObjReg4), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(3), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg5), Mem(ObjReg7)
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(0)
        modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(5000)
        modifyVar: (DIV), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(90)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(12), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ObjReg4), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(2), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg5), Mem(ObjReg7)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(5000)
        modifyVar: (DIV), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(90)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(3), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ObjReg4), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(3), Mem(ObjReg7)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg5), Mem(ObjReg7)
      endElse: 
    endElse: 
  endElse: 
  storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ObjReg6), (ENEMY), Mem(SpeedX)
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(-50000)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(32000)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(32000)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(-32000)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(-32000)
  endIf: 
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(-2), Mem(ObjReg7)
  modifyVar: (DIV), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(1)
  modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(0)
  modifyVar: (DIV), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(1)
  moveCameraTargetCameraOnBlend: 4, 30, s32'brake'
  moveCameraBasePosOffset: 2, 59, 2, 56, 2, 57, 0, 8, 0, 400, 0, 0, s32'linear', s32'linear'
  modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ObjReg3), Val(30)
  modifyVar: (DIV), Mem(ObjReg3), Val(100)
  moveCameraTargetPosOffset: 2, 60, 2, 56, 2, 58, 0, 8, 0, 400, 0, 0, s32'linear', s32'linear'
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnHighGuard'
  ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(DmgAtkAngleGuardForce), Val(2147483647)
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(DmgAtkAngleGuardForce), Val(45)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(DmgAtkAngleGuardForce), Val(-45)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(2)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    posTypeToVar: (SELF), (DAMAGE), Val(0), Mem(ActReg2)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Mem(ActReg0)
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(DmgAtkAngle), Val(45)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Mem(ActReg0)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(DmgAtkAngle), Val(-45)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(2)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endElse: 
endSubroutine:

  endUpon: 
endSubroutine:

      resetMotionBlurAmount: 
    endIf:

    velocityXPercent: 75
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnBurst'
  recoveryState: 
  haltMomentum: 1
  enableSuperArmor: 1
  superArmorArmorBreak: 1
  ignorePushback: 1
  ignoreSlowdown: 1
  suikomare: 0
  checkCurrentStateEntryName: s32'CmnMaximumBurst'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    voiceLine: s16'vxxx115'
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(11)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(33)
    modifyBurstGauge: -10000
  endIf: 
  else: 
    voiceLine: s16'vxxx114'
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(11)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(40)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(28)
    modifyBurstGauge: -15000
  endElse: 
  warp: (SELF), (PLAYER), Val(0), Val(200000), Mem(ActReg0)
  velocityYPercentEachFrame: 95
  upon: (IDLING)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Mem(ActReg0)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'_Bakuhatsu'
      haltMomentum: 1
      zLine: (NEAR_DISTANCE), 5
      checkCurrentStateEntryName: s32'CmnMaximumBurst'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        createObject: s32'cmn_BurstObjGold', (PLAYER)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        createObject: s32'cmn_BurstObjBlue', (PLAYER)
      endElse: 
      upon: (SIGNAL_NAME)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL_NAME)
        checkSignalName: s32'cmn_burst'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL0)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(1)
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Mem(ActReg1)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'_Drop'
      defaultGravity: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Mem(ActReg2)
      ifNot: Mem(ActReg3)
        enableSuperArmor: 0
        setStrikeInvulnerable: 0
        setThrowInvulnerable: 1
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  upon: (FALL_SPEED)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (FALL_SPEED)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
    landingAutoAction: 0
    upon: (TOUCH_GROUND)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'landing'
      ifNot: Mem(ActReg3)
        enableSuperArmor: 0
        damageToAir: 0
        setStrikeInvulnerable: 0
        setThrowInvulnerable: 0
      endIf: 
      upon: (IDLING)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(9)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
          jumpToState: s32'_NEUTRAL'
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnThrowPosition_F_Wall'
  ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
    ifNot: Mem(Dir)
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg0)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActReg3)
        upon: (IDLING)
          modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg2), Val(-1)
          if: Mem(ActReg2)
            modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(ActReg3), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg4)
            modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg4)
            modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ActReg3), Mem(ActReg4)
          endIf: 
          else: 
            clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
            storeValue: Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg0)
          endElse: 
        endUpon: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(-1)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg0)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActReg3)
        upon: (IDLING)
          modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg2), Val(-1)
          if: Mem(ActReg2)
            modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(ActReg3), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg4)
            modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg4)
            modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ActReg3), Mem(ActReg4)
          endIf: 
          else: 
            clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
            storeValue: Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg0)
          endElse: 
        endUpon: 
      endIf: 
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

  stackObject: (STACK0), (PREVIOUS)
  ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Mem(FuncArg0)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg6), Mem(FuncArg1)
    if: Mem(Dir)
      modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Val(-1)
      modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg5), Val(-1)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg6)
        storeValue: Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg6)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg5)
        storeValue: Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg5)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg5)
        storeValue: Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg5)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg6)
        storeValue: Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg6)
      endIf: 
    endElse: 
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Mem(FuncArg2)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg6), Mem(FuncArg3)
    ifTrueInObject: (STACK0), Mem(Dir)
      modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Val(-1)
      modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg5), Val(-1)
      storeValueFromObject: (STACK0), Mem(ActReg5), (SELF), Mem(ActReg5)
      storeValueFromObject: (STACK0), Mem(ActReg6), (SELF), Mem(ActReg6)
      ifOperationInObject: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), (STACK0), Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg6)
        storeValueFromObject: (STACK0), Mem(PosXRaw), (STACK0), Mem(ActReg6)
      endIf: 
      ifOperationInObject: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), (STACK0), Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg5)
        storeValueFromObject: (STACK0), Mem(PosXRaw), (STACK0), Mem(ActReg5)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      storeValueFromObject: (STACK0), Mem(ActReg5), (SELF), Mem(ActReg5)
      storeValueFromObject: (STACK0), Mem(ActReg6), (SELF), Mem(ActReg6)
      ifOperationInObject: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), (STACK0), Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg5)
        storeValueFromObject: (STACK0), Mem(PosXRaw), (STACK0), Mem(ActReg5)
      endIf: 
      ifOperationInObject: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), (STACK0), Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(ActReg6)
        storeValueFromObject: (STACK0), Mem(PosXRaw), (STACK0), Mem(ActReg6)
      endIf: 
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmnInitializeThrowBaseAndTarget', Val(-960000), Val(960000), Val(-960000), Val(960000)
    moveCameraTargetCameraOnBlend: 23, 8, s32'accel_brake'

    focalFarBlurSize: -1, 5, 10
    resetDiffusion: 1, 1
    setDiffusionLuminance: -1, 1400, 40
    setDiffusionThreshold: -1, 0, 40
    upon: (AFTER_FRAME_STEP)
      runOnObject: (STACK0)
        setPosXBetweenObject: 3, 22
        setPosYBetweenObject: 3, 22
      endRunOnObject: 
      ifOperationInObject: (IS_GREATER), (STACK0), Mem(PosXRaw), Val(960000)
        runOnObject: (STACK0)
          storeValue: Mem(PosXRaw), Val(960000)
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperationInObject: (IS_LESSER), (STACK0), Mem(PosXRaw), Val(-960000)
        runOnObject: (STACK0)
          storeValue: Mem(PosXRaw), Val(-960000)
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
      warp: (STACK0), (PLAYER), Val(0), Val(0), Val(8)
      checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'AirThrowExe'
      ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (AFTER_FRAME_STEP)
        gotoLabelRequests: s32'end'
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
    upon: (SIGNAL0)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL0)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (AFTER_FRAME_STEP)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'end'
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'null', 180
  endLabel: 
  beginLabel: s32'end'
  sprite: s32'null', 20
  moveCameraStop: 20, s32'brake'
  moveCameraOrthoCurve: s32'orthoone', 0, 20, s32'orthoone'
  resetDOF: 0, 20
  resetDiffusion: 0, 20
  moveCameraTargetCameraOnBlend: 23, 20, s32'accel_brake'
  moveCameraTargetPosRate: 0, 1000, 0, 0, 0, 20, 0, 0, 0, 0, s32'brake', s32'brake'
  moveCameraFOV: 0, 65, 0, 20, 0, 0, 0, 0, s32'accel_brake', s32'brake'
endState: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnCam_Initialize'
  runOnObject: (PLAYER)
    slowdownEndOnHit: 1
  endRunOnObject: 
  ignoreSlowdown: 1
  callSubroutine: s32'cmn_cam_delete_on_rc'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmn_cam_delete_on_wsb'
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnCam_InitializeBase'
  linkCommonPawn: 
  if: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
    moveCameraTargetPosRate: 0, 0, 0, 1000, 0, 0, 0, 100, 0, 0, s32'accel_brake', s32'accel_brake'
    moveCameraTargetRotRate: 0, 0, 0, 1000, 0, 0, 0, 100, 0, 0, s32'accel_brake', s32'linear'
    moveCameraSplinePosRate: 0, 0, 0, 1000, 0, 0, 0, 100, 0, 0, s32'linear', s32'brake'
  endIf: 
  else: 
    moveCameraReset: 
    resetCamera: 
  endElse: 
  moveCameraBasePosObject: (SELF)
  sendSignalToAction: s32'cmnHiCounterCamera', (SIGNAL9)
  ignoreSlowdown: 1
  createObject: s32'cmnCam_Singleton', (PLAYER)
  upon: (ACTION_END)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnCam_ClearCamInterrupt'
    sendSignalToAction: s32'cmnCam_Singleton', (SIGNAL0)
    deactivateObjectById: (STACK0)
  endUpon: 
  upon: (SIGNAL_NAME)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL_NAME)
    checkSignalName: s32'DeleteCamera'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      callSubroutine: s32'cmnCam_ClearCamInterrupt'
      deactivateObjectById: (SELF)
      deactivateObjectById: (STACK0)
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  upon: (WALL_BREAK)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnCam_ClearCamInterrupt'
    deactivateObjectById: (SELF)
    deactivateObjectById: (STACK0)
    createObject: s32'cmnCam_ReturnToDefault', (PLAYER)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnGlareDelete'
  endUpon: 
  upon: (WALL)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnCam_ClearCamInterrupt'
    deactivateObjectById: (SELF)
    deactivateObjectById: (STACK0)
    createObject: s32'cmnCam_ReturnToDefault', (PLAYER)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnGlareDelete'
  endUpon: 
  upon: (GUARD)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnCam_ClearCamInterrupt'
    deactivateObjectById: (SELF)
    deactivateObjectById: (STACK0)
    createObject: s32'cmnCam_ReturnToDefault', (PLAYER)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnGlareDelete'
  endUpon: 
  upon: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnCam_ClearCamInterrupt'
    deactivateObjectById: (SELF)
    deactivateObjectById: (STACK0)
    createObject: s32'cmnCam_ReturnToDefault', (PLAYER)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnGlareDelete'
  endUpon: 
  upon: (BEFORE_EXIT)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnCam_CommonCameraEnd'
    if: Mem(BattleDoing)
      ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
        resetDOF: 0, 20
        resetDiffusion: 0, 20
        resetSaturation: 0, 20
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  if: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
    moveCameraFOV: 0, 65, 0, 0, 0, 500, 0, 0, s32'accel_brake', s32'brake'
    resetMotionBlurAmount: 
  endIf: 
  callSubroutine: s32'cmn_cam_delete_on_rc'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnCamCounterSlowSettings'
  moveCameraStart: 
endSubroutine: 

beginState: s32'cmnCam_FinishTimeOut'
  sprite: s32'null', 130
  sprite: s32'null', 20
  ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
    focalDistance: 700, 0, 0
    focalRegion: 0, 0, 0
    focalNearTransition: 0, 0, 0
    focalFarTransition: 500, 0, 0
    focalNearBlurSize: 0, 0, 0
    focalFarBlurSize: 40, 0, 0

    hideUI: 0
  endIf: 
endState:

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnCam_ClearCamInterrupt'
  clearRegisteredUponCode: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK)
  clearRegisteredUponCode: (WALL_BREAK)
  clearRegisteredUponCode: (WALL)
  clearRegisteredUponCode: (ACTION_END)
  clearRegisteredUponCode: (AFTER_FRAME_STEP)
  clearRegisteredUponCode: (FRAME_STEP)
  clearRegisteredUponCode: (AFTER_EXIT)
  clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL_NAME)
  clearRegisteredUponCode: (ENEMY_RECEIVE_ATTACK_AFTER_FIX_PARAM)
  sendSignalToAction: s32'cmnCam_Singleton', (SIGNAL0)
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnCameraSettings'
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg3), Val(0)
    sendSignalToAction: s32'cmnCam_Singleton', (SIGNAL1)
    ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
      moveCameraReset: 
      resetCamera: 
      deactivateObjectByNameAll: s32'cmnHiCounterCamera'
    endIf: 
    runOnObject: (PLAYER)
      resetMotionBlurAmount: 
    endRunOnObject: 
    runOnObject: (ENEMY)
      resetMotionBlurAmount: 
    endRunOnObject: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg3), Val(1)
    cinesco: 0
    hideUI: 0
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnGlareDelete'
    resetDOF: 0, 40
    resetSaturation: 0, 20
    resetDiffusion: 0, 40
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginState: s32'cmnCam_Singleton'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg0), Val(0)
    moveCameraOrthoCurve: s32'orthozero', 0, 500, s32'orthoone'
    deactivateObjectByNameExceptSelf: s32'cmnCam_Singleton'
    runOnObject: (ENEMY)
      deactivateObjectByName: s32'cmnCam_Singleton'
    endRunOnObject: 
    upon: (SIGNAL0)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL0)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg0), Val(1)
      deactivateObjectById: (SELF)
    endUpon: 
    upon: (SIGNAL1)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL1)
      deactivateObjectById: (SELF)
      sendSignalName: 2, s32'DeleteCamera', 0
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (ON_DELETE)
      resetMotionBlurAmount: 
    endUpon: 
    upon: (ON_DELETE)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (ON_DELETE)
      if: Mem(ObjReg0)
        moveCameraOrthoCurve: s32'orthodefault', 0, 0, s32'orthoone'
      endIf: 
      else: 
        sendSignalName: 2, s32'DeleteCamera', 0
      endElse: 
      resetMotionBlurAmount: 
    endUpon: 
    ignoreSuperFreeze: 1
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'null', 500
endState:

beginSubroutine: s32'cmn_cam_delete_on_rc'
  upon: (AFTER_EXIT)
    upon: (FRAME_STEP)
      checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActRomanCancel'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        callSubroutine: s32'cmnCam_ClearCamInterrupt'
        deactivateObjectById: (SELF)
        deactivateObjectById: (STACK0)
        ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
          createObject: s32'cmnCam_ReturnToDefault', (PLAYER)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmn_cam_delete_on_wsb'
  upon: (WALL_BREAK)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (WALL_BREAK)
    deactivateObjectById: (SELF)
    moveCameraReset: 
    moveCameraOrthoCurve: s32'orthozero', 0, 0, s32'orthoone'
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmn_cam_delete_on_finish'
  clearRegisteredUponCode: (WALL_BREAK)
  deactivateObjectById: (SELF)
  moveCameraReset: 
  moveCameraOrthoCurve: s32'orthozero', 0, 1, s32'orthoone'
  resetMotionBlurAmount: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmn_vertical_offset'
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(-3)
    pushScreenOffset: 0, -240000, 0, 0
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(-2)
    pushScreenOffset: 0, -160000, 0, 0
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(-1)
    pushScreenOffset: 0, -80000, 0, 0
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(1)
    pushScreenOffset: 0, 80000, 0, 0
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(2)
    pushScreenOffset: 0, 160000, 0, 0
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(3)
    pushScreenOffset: 0, 240000, 0, 0
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

  ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)

      setMotionBlurAmount: 50
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(2)

    endIf:

      setMotionBlurAmount: 100
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(4)
      setMotionBlurAmount: 150
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(5)
      setMotionBlurAmount: 200
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(6)
      setMotionBlurAmount: 300
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(7)
      setMotionBlurAmount: 400
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(8)
      setMotionBlurAmount: 500
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(9)
      setMotionBlurAmount: 700
    endIf:

    endIf: 
  endIf:

beginSubroutine: s32'cmn_FloatDamage'
  haltMomentum: 1
  if: Mem(IsFloatDmgHead)
    upon: (IDLING)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(1)
        physicsXImpulse: 0, -15000
        velocityXPercentEachFrame: 90
        physicsYImpulse: 0, 20000
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(3)
        physicsYImpulse: 0, 7500
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(7)
        physicsYImpulse: 0, 2500
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(13)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
        velocityXPercentEachFrame: 80
        physicsYImpulse: 0, 0
        setGravity: 4000
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(IsFloatDmgBody)
    physicsXImpulse: 0, -20000
    velocityXPercentEachFrame: 80
    setGravity: 1000
    checkLastAttackHitStateName: 3, s32'NmlAtk5E'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      upon: (FALL_SPEED)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (FALL_SPEED)
        ignoreSpeedTime: 1
      endUpon: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  upon: (TOUCH_GROUND)
    createArgScale: 0, 750
    createParticleWithArg2: s32'bg_down_default', (BACK_05_BODY)
    velocityXPercentEachFrame: 85
    if: Mem(IsFloatDmgHead)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'head_landing'
      storeValue: Mem(StunTime), Val(14)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(0)
      upon: (IDLING)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(8)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
          enableBlock: 1
          enableInvalidCombo: 1
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endIf: 
    if: Mem(IsFloatDmgBody)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'body_landing'
      storeValue: Mem(StunTime), Val(17)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(0)
      upon: (IDLING)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(7)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
          enableBlock: 1
          enableInvalidCombo: 1
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'cmn_GorogoroBGParticle'
  setEventTrigger: (TIMER), 1
  upon: (TIMER)
    createParticle: s32'cmn_landcrack', (PLAYER)
    upon: (IDLING)
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(16)
        createParticle: s32'cmn_landcrack', (PLAYER)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(0)
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmn_Jitabata'
  upon: (IDLING)
    if: Mem(ActReg0)
      ifNot: Mem(ActReg1)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(5)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Val(13)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(2)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(9)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Val(18)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(3)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(13)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Val(23)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Mem(ActReg3)
        enableBlock: 1
        enableInvalidCombo: 1
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Mem(ActReg4)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
        jumpToState: s32'_NEUTRAL'
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine:

endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmn_Down2Stand'

    storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(15)
  endIf: 
  else: 
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(25)
  endElse: 
  upon: (IDLING)

      setCrouch: 1
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Mem(ActReg0)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
      setCrouch: 0
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnOnWSBCalc'
  runOnObject: (ENEMY)
    estimateWallBreakDamage: (ENEMY), Val(50), Val(75)
  endRunOnObject: 
  if: Mem(IsDeadWSBEstimateDmg)
    runOnObject: (ENEMY)
      wallBreakDamage: (ENEMY)
    endRunOnObject: 
  endIf: 
  isObjectActive: (ATTACKER)
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    ifTrueInObject: (ATTACKER), Mem(IsPlayer)
      runOnObject: (ENEMY)
        sendValuesToObject: 0, 1, 2, 319
        createObjectWithArg: s32'cmnWorldSideBreakObj', (PLAYER)
      endRunOnObject: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      runOnObject: (ENEMY)
        sendValuesToObject: 0, 0, 2, 319
        createObjectWithArg: s32'cmnWorldSideBreakObj', (PLAYER)
      endRunOnObject: 
      runOnObject: (ATTACKER)
        superFreeze: 0, 119, 1, 1
      endRunOnObject: 
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    runOnObject: (ENEMY)
      sendValuesToObject: 0, 0, 2, 319
      createObjectWithArg: s32'cmnWorldSideBreakObj', (PLAYER)
    endRunOnObject: 
  endElse: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnWorldSideBreak_Position'
  runOnObject: (PLAYER)
    setNoCollision: 0
    landingAutoAction: 0
  endRunOnObject: 
  calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_RAW), (PLAYER), (PLAYER), (ENEMY), (PLAYER)
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(Tmp), Val(500000)
    if: Mem(SentToObject0)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      runOnObject: (PLAYER)
        storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaActReg0), Val(-500000)
      endRunOnObject: 
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Val(-1), Mem(EnemyDiffY), Mem(CmnCharaActReg1)
    calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_RAW), (PLAYER), (PLAYER), (ENEMY), (PLAYER)
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(Tmp), Val(750000)
      runOnObject: (PLAYER)
        storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaActReg0), Val(-750000)
      endRunOnObject: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      runOnObject: (PLAYER)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Val(-1), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Mem(CmnCharaActReg0)
      endRunOnObject: 
    endElse: 
  endElse: 
  ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(IsLand)
    runOnObject: (PLAYER)
      moveToPosType: (ENEMY), (PLAYER_LAND)
    endRunOnObject: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    runOnObject: (PLAYER)
      moveToPosType: (ENEMY), (PLAYER)
    endRunOnObject: 
  endElse: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageSplitCount), Val(3)
    runOnObject: (PLAYER)
      modifyVar: (DIV), Mem(CmnCharaActReg0), Val(2)
      modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(CmnCharaActReg0), Val(17), Mem(CmnCharaActReg2)
      modifyVar: (DIV), Mem(CmnCharaActReg2), Val(10)
    endRunOnObject: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(WSBMoveDir), Val(1)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(CmnCharaActReg0), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(WSBMoveDir), Val(-1)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(CmnCharaActReg0), Val(-1)
  endIf: 
  runOnObject: (PLAYER)
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(PosXRaw), Mem(CmnCharaActReg0)
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(PosY), Mem(CmnCharaActReg1)
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(PosZ), Mem(CmnCharaActReg2)
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(AngleY), Mem(CmnCharaActReg7)
  endRunOnObject: 
  runOnObject: (PLAYER)
    enableRomanCancel: 0
  endRunOnObject: 
  runOnObject: (ENEMY)
    enableBurst: 0
  endRunOnObject: 
endSubroutine: 

beginState: s32'cmnWorldSideBreakObj'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    runOnObject: (PLAYER)
      hitStopTime: 
      ignoreSuperFreezeFromAlly: 0
      ignoreSuperFreeze: 0
      hitStopTime: 
      invulnForce: 1
      storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg3), Val(1)
      superFreeze: 0, 119, 1, 1
      timeSlow: 0
    endRunOnObject: 
    runOnObject: (ENEMY)
      hitStopTime: 
      ignoreSuperFreezeFromAlly: 0
      ignoreSuperFreeze: 0
      invulnForce: 1
      storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg3), Val(1)
      superFreeze: 0, 119, 1, 1
      timeSlow: 0
    endRunOnObject: 
    storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ActReg7), (ENEMY), Mem(PosXRaw)
    particleSlowdown: 60, 750
    if: Mem(SentToObject0)
      stopLinkObject: 3
      linkObjPosition: 3
      runOnObject: (PLAYER)
        ignoreSuperFreeze: 0
        ignoreSuperFreezeFromAlly: 0
        cmnSfx: s32'SE_BTL_CMN_Wall_PreCrash_2'
      endRunOnObject: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      moveToObject: (ENEMY)
      stopLinkObject: 22
      linkObjPosition: 22
      cmnSfx: s32'SE_BTL_CMN_Wall_PreCrash_2'
    endElse: 
    ifNotInObject: (ENEMY), Mem(HitPoint)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    resetDOF: 0, 10
    resetSaturation: 0, 10
    resetDiffusion: 0, 10
    pauseTimer: 1
    ignoreSlowdown: 1
    timeSlow: 0
  endUpon: 
  upon: (ON_DELETE)
    wallBreakSceneEnd: 
    runOnObject: (ENEMY)
      storeValue: Mem(WSBPoint), Val(0)
    endRunOnObject: 
    runOnObject: (PLAYER)
      storeValue: Mem(WSBPoint), Val(0)
    endRunOnObject: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'null', 2147483647
  ifNot: Mem(ObjReg6)
    superFreeze: 9, 119, 60, 60
  endIf: 
  else: 
    superFreeze: 9, 119, 1, 1
  endElse: 
  upon: (AFTER_FRAME_STEP_EX)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnWorldSideBreak_Base'
  endUpon: 
endState: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnWorldSideBreak_Type'
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(WSBNextHeight), Val(2184), Mem(ActReg2)
  storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ActReg3), (ENEMY), Mem(PosY)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Mem(ActReg3), Mem(ActReg2), Mem(ActReg4)
  storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ActReg5), (ENEMY), Mem(WSBPattern)
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg5), Val(1)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(WSBNextHeight), Val(0)
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(ActReg4), Val(250000)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(WSBNextHeight), Val(0)
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(ActReg4), Val(0)
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(ActReg4), Val(250000)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
        endIf: 
        else: 
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      else: 
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(2)
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(WSBNextHeight), Val(0)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg5), Val(2)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(WSBNextHeight), Val(0)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(2)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(WSBNextHeight), Val(0)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(2)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(WSBNextHeight), Val(0)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(2)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg5), Val(3)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(WSBNextHeight), Val(0)
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(ActReg4), Val(250000)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(4)
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(WSBNextHeight), Val(0)
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(ActReg4), Val(250000)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(4)
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(WSBNextHeight), Val(0)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifNot: Mem(ActReg1)
    debugLogForScript: s32'cmnWSB_Type', 2, 46
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginState: s32'cmnWSB_FinishCamera'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    ignoreSuperFreeze: 1
    linkCommonPawn: 
    ignoreZLine: 1
    hideUI: 1
    cinesco: 1
    flipDirection: 
    resetSaturation: 1, 1
    setPostProcessSaturation: -1, 800, 40
    resetDiffusion: 1, 1
    setDiffusionLuminance: -1, 1400, 50
    setDiffusionThreshold: -1, 0, 50
    resetDOF: 1, 1
    focalDistance: -1, 700, 0
    focalRegion: -1, 0, 0
    focalNearTransition: -1, 0, 0
    focalFarTransition: -1, 500, 0
    focalNearBlurSize: -1, 0, 0
    focalFarBlurSize: -1, 10, 10
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnGlareDelete'
    createGlareEffect: 1
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Mem(Tmp)
    setGlareColor: 2, 45, 0, 127, 0, 255, 0, 255, 0, 255
    setGlareScale: 2, 45, 0, 1200, 0, 1200
    ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(Dir)
      setGlareOffset: 2, 45, 0, -300000, 0, -300000
    endIf: 
    else: 
      setGlareOffset: 2, 45, 0, 300000, 0, -300000
    endElse: 
    setEventTrigger: (TIMER), 72
    upon: (TIMER)
      resetDOF: 0, 40
      resetSaturation: 0, 20
      resetDiffusion: 0, 40
      removeGlareEffect: 2, 45
    endUpon: 
    upon: (FRAME_STEP)
      runOnObject: (PLAYER)
        zLine: (FAR_DISTANCE), 5
      endRunOnObject: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'null', 1
  resetCamera: 
  moveCameraReset: 
  moveCameraBasePosObject: (SELF)
  moveCameraSpline: s32'cmn_WorldSideBreak_finish', 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, s32'linear'
  moveCameraSpline: s32'cmn_WorldSideBreak_finish', 0, 0, 0, 1000, 0, 300, s32'linear'
  moveCameraSplinePosRate: 0, 1000, 0, 1000, 0, 0, 0, 1000, 0, 0, s32'linear', s32'linear'
  moveCameraTargetCameraOnBlend: 3, 0, s32'brake'
  moveCameraTargetPosOffset: 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 135000, 0, 0, 0, 1000, 0, 0, s32'linear', s32'linear'
  moveCameraTargetPercent: 0, 100, 0, 100, 0, 0, 0, 1000, 0, 0, s32'linear', s32'linear'
  moveCameraTargetPosRate: 0, 1000, 0, 1000, 0, 0, 0, 1000, 0, 0, s32'linear', s32'linear'
  moveCameraTargetRotRate: 0, 1000, 0, 1000, 0, 0, 0, 1000, 0, 0, s32'linear', s32'linear'
  moveCameraTargetRotRoll: 0, -10000, 0, -15000, 0, 30, 0, 30, 0, 60, s32'linear', s32'linear'
  moveCameraFOV: 0, 80, 0, 60, 0, 1000, 0, 0, s32'linear', s32'linear'
  moveCameraTargetPosOffset: 0, 0, 0, 100000, 0, 135000, 0, 0, 0, 1000, 0, 0, s32'linear', s32'linear'
  moveCameraStart:

  sprite: s32'null', 10

  moveCameraBasePosObject: (ENEMY)

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnWorldSideBreak_Action_Master'
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
    runOnObject: (PLAYER)
      jumpToState: s32'WSB_Master_Slide'
    endRunOnObject: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(2)
    runOnObject: (PLAYER)
      jumpToState: s32'WSB_Master_Up'
    endRunOnObject: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
    runOnObject: (PLAYER)
      jumpToState: s32'WSB_Master_Down'
    endRunOnObject: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(4)
    runOnObject: (PLAYER)
      jumpToState: s32'WSB_Master_Bound'
    endRunOnObject: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnWorldSideBreak_Action_Slave'
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
    runOnObject: (ENEMY)
      jumpToStateKeepDamage: s32'WSB_Slave_Slide'
    endRunOnObject: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(2)
    runOnObject: (ENEMY)
      jumpToStateKeepDamage: s32'WSB_Slave_Up'
    endRunOnObject: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
    runOnObject: (ENEMY)
      jumpToStateKeepDamage: s32'WSB_Slave_Down'
    endRunOnObject: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(4)
    runOnObject: (ENEMY)
      jumpToStateKeepDamage: s32'WSB_Slave_Bound'
    endRunOnObject: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Action_Default'
  playerActionInitializeByCategory: 60, 0
  invulnForce: 1
  enableRomanCancelMove: 0
  haltMomentum: 1
  resetMotionBlurAmount: 
  upon: (BEFORE_EXIT)
    deactivateObjectByName: s32'cmnWorldSideBreakObj'
    setDepth: 0
    setDepthSpeed: 0, 0
    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg7), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg3), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(WSBPoint), Val(0)
    moveRewriteMode: 1
    addMove: s32'WSB_Master_Wait'
      addMoveFlag: 120
      removeMoveFlag: (NONE)
    endMove: 
    deactivateObjectByName: s32'cmnWSBDummy'
    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg19), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg20), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg21), Val(0)
  endUpon: 
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Action_LandingHeight'
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Action_Master_Default'
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageSplitCount), Val(6)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageOffsetRadius), Val(4500)
      setAngleY: 35000
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageOffsetRadius), Val(8000)
      setAngleY: 35000
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageSplitCount), Val(3)
    setAngleY: 70000
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(WSBMoveDir), Val(0)
    faceRight: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(WSBMoveDir), Val(0)
    faceLeft: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Action_Slave_Default'
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageSplitCount), Val(6)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageOffsetRadius), Val(4500)
      setAngleY: -35000
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageOffsetRadius), Val(8000)
      setAngleY: -35000
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageSplitCount), Val(3)
    setAngleY: -70000
  endIf: 
  storeValue: Mem(TumbleTime), Val(1)
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Master_Slide'
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageSplitCount), Val(6)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageOffsetRadius), Val(1500)
      callSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Master_Slide_6'
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageOffsetRadius), Val(4500)
      callSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Master_Slide_6_4500'
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageOffsetRadius), Val(8000)
      callSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Master_Slide_6_8000'
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageSplitCount), Val(3)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageOffsetRadius), Val(4500)
      callSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Master_Slide_3_4500'
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageOffsetRadius), Val(21000)
      callSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Master_Slide_3_21000'
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Master_Slide_6'
    debugLogForScript: s32'cmnWSB_Master_Slide_Error', 0, 0
  endIf: 
  else: 
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(0)
  endElse: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Slave_Slide'
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageSplitCount), Val(6)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageOffsetRadius), Val(1500)
      callSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Slave_Slide_6'
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
    endIf:

  endElse: 
  voiceLine: s16'vxxx003'
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Master_Up'
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageSplitCount), Val(6)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageOffsetRadius), Val(1500)

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Master_Slide_6'
  gotoLabelRequests: s32'dash'
  moveToObject: (ENEMY)
  addPositionX: 0, -1500000
  setPositionY: 0
  landingHeight: 0
  physicsXImpulse: 0, 100000
  upon: (SIGNAL_NAME)
    checkSignalName: s32'WSB_Slide'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL_NAME)
      moveToObject: (ENEMY)
      landingHeight: 0
      addPositionX: 0, -500000
      warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(100000), Val(0), Val(16)
      setDepth: 0
      setAngleY: 0
      upon: (IDLING)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(15)
          gotoLabelRequests: s32'brake'
          warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(150000), Val(0), Val(5)
          createParticleWithArg: s32'bg_dashstart', (FRONT_3_BODY)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(20)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
          haltMomentum: 1
          setPositionXInBattle: 150000
          createParticleWithArg: s32'bg_dashbrake', (PLAYER)
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  resetMotionBlurAmount: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Slave_Slide_6'
  gotoLabelRequests: s32'loop'
  createObject: s32'cmnWSB_Camera_Slide_6', (PLAYER)
  haltMomentum: 1
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(30)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(PosY), Val(10), Mem(ActReg1)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(1092000)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(2184000)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Val(500000)
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(0)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(-1)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg2)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg2)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg3)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg3)
  endIf: 
  warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Mem(ActReg4), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg0)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(SpeedY), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActReg5)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(-1), Mem(ActReg6)
  modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ActReg0)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(ActReg5), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(Gravity)
  modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(Gravity), Val(2)
  upon: (FALL_SPEED)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (FALL_SPEED)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActionTime), Mem(ActReg6)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg6), Val(-1), Mem(ActReg7)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ActReg7)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(PosY), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(Gravity)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(Gravity), Val(2)
    upon: (IDLING)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(20)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActionTime), Mem(ActReg6)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg6), Val(-1), Mem(ActReg7)
        modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ActReg7)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(PosY), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(Gravity)
        modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(Gravity), Val(2)
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
    landingHeight: 0
    upon: (TOUCH_GROUND)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'landing'
      haltMomentum: 1
      warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(-700000), Val(0), Val(15)
      effectForDownLv2: (BACK_2_BODY), 1, 0
      effectForDownLv3: (BACK_2_BODY), 1, 0
      cameraShake: s32'ShakeTateYoko', 500, 0, 10, 5
      sendSignalName: 22, s32'WSB_Slide', 0
      cmnSfx: s32'SE_BTL_CMN_Down_Def_Stone_M'
      voiceLine: s16'vxxx109'
      upon: (IDLING)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(10)
          createArgDirection: 1
          createParticleWithArg: s32'bg_dashstart', (BACK_1_BODY)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(15)
          if: Mem(HitPoint)
            if: Mem(CmnCharaReg7)
              warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(-750000), Val(0), Val(5)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'brake'
            endIf: 
            else: 
              warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(-775000), Val(0), Val(5)
              jumpToStateKeepDamage: s32'CmnActKorogari'
            endElse: 
          endIf: 
          else: 
            jumpToStateKeepDamage: s32'CmnActKorogari'
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(20)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
          setPositionXInBattle: -750000
          haltMomentum: 1
          createArgDirection: 1
          createParticleWithArg: s32'bg_dashbrake', (PLAYER)
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine:

  upon: (FRAME_STEP)
    moveToObject: (ENEMY)

    setNoCollision: 0
  endUpon: 
  upon: (SIGNAL_NAME)
    checkSignalName: s32'WSB_Up'

      clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL_NAME)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (FRAME_STEP)
      displayModel: 1
      setNoCollision: 1
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'jump'
      moveToObject: (ENEMY)
      landingHeight: 0
      addPositionX: 0, -1250000
      setPositionY: 1750000
      warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(100000), Val(0), Val(16)
      setDepth: 0
      setAngleY: 0
      upon: (FALL_SPEED)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (FALL_SPEED)

          gotoLabelRequests: s32'landing'
          warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(150000), Val(0), Val(5)
          upon: (IDLING)
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(5)
              clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
              haltMomentum: 1
              setPositionXInBattle: 150000
            endIf: 
          endUpon: 
        endUpon: 
      endUpon: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  resetMotionBlurAmount: 
endSubroutine:

  modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(PosY), Val(10), Mem(ActReg1)

  storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Val(250000)
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(0)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(-1)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg2)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg2)
  endIf:

  warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Mem(ActReg4), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg0)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(SpeedY), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActReg5)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(-1), Mem(ActReg6)
  modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ActReg0)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(ActReg5), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(Gravity)
  modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(Gravity), Val(2)
  upon: (FALL_SPEED)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (FALL_SPEED)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActionTime), Mem(ActReg6)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg6), Val(-1), Mem(ActReg7)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ActReg7)

    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(Gravity), Val(2)

      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(50)

        modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg6), Val(-1), Mem(ActReg7)
        modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ActReg7)

          createArgDirection: 1
          createParticleWithArg: s32'bg_dashstart', (BACK_1_BODY)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(15)

            if: Mem(CmnCharaReg7)
              warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(-750000), Val(0), Val(5)

            endIf:

            endElse: 
          endIf:

          endElse:

          setPositionXInBattle: -750000
          haltMomentum: 1
          createArgDirection: 1
          createParticleWithArg: s32'bg_dashbrake', (PLAYER)
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endUpon:

      setDepth: 0

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Slave_Bound_6_4500'
  gotoLabelRequests: s32'gorogoro'
  createObject: s32'cmnWSB_Camera_Bound_6_L', (PLAYER)
  resetMotionBlurAmount: 
  haltMomentum: 1
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(90)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(PosY), Val(10), Mem(ActReg1)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(21840000)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(43680000)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Val(500000)
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(0)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(-1)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg2)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg2)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg3)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg3)
  endIf: 
  warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Mem(ActReg4), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg0)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(SpeedY), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActReg5)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(-1), Mem(ActReg6)
  modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ActReg0)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(ActReg5), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(Gravity)
  modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(Gravity), Val(2)
  upon: (FALL_SPEED)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (FALL_SPEED)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActionTime), Mem(ActReg6)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg6), Val(-1), Mem(ActReg7)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ActReg7)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(PosY), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(Gravity)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(Gravity), Val(2)
    upon: (IDLING)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(80)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActionTime), Mem(ActReg6)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg6), Val(-1), Mem(ActReg7)
        modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ActReg7)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(PosY), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(Gravity)
        modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(Gravity), Val(2)
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
    landingHeight: 0
    upon: (TOUCH_GROUND)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'landing'
      haltMomentum: 1
      warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(-700000), Val(0), Val(15)
      setAngleY: 0
      effectForDownLv2: (BACK_2_BODY), 1, 0
      effectForDownLv3: (BACK_2_BODY), 1, 0
      cameraShake: s32'ShakeTateYoko', 500, 0, 10, 5
      sendSignalName: 22, s32'WSB_Bound', 0
      cmnSfx: s32'SE_BTL_CMN_Down_Def_Stone_M'
      voiceLine: s16'vxxx109'
      upon: (IDLING)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(10)
          createArgDirection: 1
          createParticleWithArg: s32'bg_dashstart', (BACK_1_BODY)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(15)
          if: Mem(HitPoint)
            if: Mem(CmnCharaReg7)
              warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(-750000), Val(0), Val(5)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'brake'
            endIf: 
            else: 
              warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(-775000), Val(0), Val(5)
              jumpToStateKeepDamage: s32'CmnActKorogari'
            endElse: 
          endIf: 
          else: 
            jumpToStateKeepDamage: s32'CmnActKorogari'
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(20)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
          setPositionXInBattle: -750000
          haltMomentum: 1
          createArgDirection: 1
          createParticleWithArg: s32'bg_dashbrake', (PLAYER)
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  setDepthSpeed: 0, 46666
  upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(PosZ), Val(-46666)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
      setDepthSpeed: 0, 0
      setDepth: 0
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine:

    setNoCollision: 0

      clearRegisteredUponCode: (FRAME_STEP)
      displayModel: 1
      setNoCollision: 1

      setDepth: 0
      setAngleY: 0

          gotoLabelRequests: s32'brake'
          warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(150000), Val(0), Val(5)
          createParticleWithArg: s32'bg_dashstart', (FRONT_3_BODY)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(20)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
          haltMomentum: 1
          setPositionXInBattle: 150000
          createParticleWithArg: s32'bg_dashbrake', (PLAYER)
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon:

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Master_Down_6_8000'
  upon: (FRAME_STEP)
    moveToObject: (ENEMY)
    displayModel: 0
    setNoCollision: 0
  endUpon: 
  upon: (SIGNAL_NAME)
    checkSignalName: s32'WSB_Down'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL_NAME)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (FRAME_STEP)
      displayModel: 1
      setNoCollision: 1
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'jump'
      moveToObject: (ENEMY)
      landingHeight: 0
      addPositionX: 0, -1250000
      setPositionY: 1750000
      warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(100000), Val(0), Val(16)
      setDepth: 0
      setAngleY: 0
      upon: (FALL_SPEED)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (FALL_SPEED)
        upon: (TOUCH_GROUND)
          gotoLabelRequests: s32'landing'
          warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(150000), Val(0), Val(5)
          upon: (IDLING)
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(5)
              clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
              haltMomentum: 1
              setPositionXInBattle: 150000
            endIf: 
          endUpon: 
        endUpon: 
      endUpon: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Slave_Down_6_8000'
  gotoLabelRequests: s32'loop'
  createObject: s32'cmnWSB_Camera_Down_6_8000', (PLAYER)
  resetMotionBlurAmount: 
  haltMomentum: 1
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(90)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(PosY), Val(10), Mem(ActReg1)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(21840000)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(43680000)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Val(500000)
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(0)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(-1)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg2)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg2)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg3)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg3)
  endIf: 
  warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Mem(ActReg4), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg0)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(SpeedY), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActReg5)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(-1), Mem(ActReg6)
  modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ActReg0)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(ActReg5), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(Gravity)
  modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(Gravity), Val(2)
  upon: (FALL_SPEED)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (FALL_SPEED)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActionTime), Mem(ActReg6)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg6), Val(-1), Mem(ActReg7)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ActReg7)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(PosY), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(Gravity)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(Gravity), Val(2)
    upon: (IDLING)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(80)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActionTime), Mem(ActReg6)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg6), Val(-1), Mem(ActReg7)
        modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ActReg7)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(PosY), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(Gravity)
        modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(Gravity), Val(2)
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
    landingHeight: 0
    upon: (TOUCH_GROUND)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'landing'
      haltMomentum: 1
      warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(-700000), Val(0), Val(15)
      setAngleY: 0
      effectForDownLv2: (BACK_2_BODY), 1, 0
      effectForDownLv3: (BACK_2_BODY), 1, 0
      cameraShake: s32'ShakeTateYoko', 500, 0, 10, 5
      sendSignalName: 22, s32'WSB_Down', 0
      cmnSfx: s32'SE_BTL_CMN_Down_Def_Stone_M'
      voiceLine: s16'vxxx109'
      upon: (IDLING)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(10)
          createArgDirection: 1
          createParticleWithArg: s32'bg_dashstart', (BACK_1_BODY)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(15)
          if: Mem(HitPoint)
            if: Mem(CmnCharaReg7)
              warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(-750000), Val(0), Val(5)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'brake'
            endIf: 
            else: 
              warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(-775000), Val(0), Val(5)
              jumpToStateKeepDamage: s32'CmnActKorogari'
            endElse: 
          endIf: 
          else: 
            jumpToStateKeepDamage: s32'CmnActKorogari'
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(20)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
          setPositionXInBattle: -750000
          haltMomentum: 1
          createArgDirection: 1
          createParticleWithArg: s32'bg_dashbrake', (PLAYER)
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  setDepthSpeed: 0, 100000
  upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(PosZ), Val(-100000)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
      setDepthSpeed: 0, 0
      setDepth: 0
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Slave_Bound_3_4500'
  gotoLabelRequests: s32'gorogoro'
  createObject: s32'cmnWSB_Camera_Bound_3', (PLAYER)
  resetMotionBlurAmount: 
  haltMomentum: 1
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(90)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(PosY), Val(10), Mem(ActReg1)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(43680000)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(87360000)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Val(500000)
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(0)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(-1)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg2)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg2)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg3)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg3)
  endIf: 
  warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Mem(ActReg4), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg0)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(SpeedY), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActReg5)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(-1), Mem(ActReg6)
  modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ActReg0)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(ActReg5), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(Gravity)
  modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(Gravity), Val(2)
  upon: (FALL_SPEED)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (FALL_SPEED)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActionTime), Mem(ActReg6)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg6), Val(-1), Mem(ActReg7)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ActReg7)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(PosY), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(Gravity)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(Gravity), Val(2)
    upon: (IDLING)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(80)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActionTime), Mem(ActReg6)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg6), Val(-1), Mem(ActReg7)
        modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ActReg7)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(PosY), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(Gravity)
        modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(Gravity), Val(2)
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
    landingHeight: 0
    upon: (TOUCH_GROUND)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'landing'
      haltMomentum: 1
      warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(-700000), Val(0), Val(15)
      setAngleY: 0
      effectForDownLv2: (BACK_2_BODY), 1, 0
      effectForDownLv3: (BACK_2_BODY), 1, 0
      cameraShake: s32'ShakeTateYoko', 500, 0, 10, 5
      sendSignalName: 22, s32'WSB_Bound', 0
      cmnSfx: s32'SE_BTL_CMN_Down_Def_Stone_M'
      voiceLine: s16'vxxx109'
      upon: (IDLING)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(10)
          createArgDirection: 1
          createParticleWithArg: s32'bg_dashstart', (BACK_1_BODY)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(15)
          if: Mem(HitPoint)
            if: Mem(CmnCharaReg7)
              warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(-750000), Val(0), Val(5)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'brake'
            endIf: 
            else: 
              warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(-775000), Val(0), Val(5)
              jumpToStateKeepDamage: s32'CmnActKorogari'
            endElse: 
          endIf: 
          else: 
            jumpToStateKeepDamage: s32'CmnActKorogari'
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(20)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
          setPositionXInBattle: -750000
          haltMomentum: 1
          createArgDirection: 1
          createParticleWithArg: s32'bg_dashbrake', (PLAYER)
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  setDepthSpeed: 0, 176666
  upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(PosZ), Val(-176666)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
      setDepthSpeed: 0, 0
      setDepth: 0
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Master_Down_3_21000'
  upon: (FRAME_STEP)
    moveToObject: (ENEMY)
    displayModel: 0
    setNoCollision: 0
  endUpon: 
  upon: (SIGNAL_NAME)
    checkSignalName: s32'WSB_Down'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL_NAME)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (FRAME_STEP)
      displayModel: 1
      setNoCollision: 1
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'jump'
      moveToObject: (ENEMY)
      landingHeight: 0
      addPositionX: 0, -1250000
      setPositionY: 1750000
      warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(100000), Val(0), Val(16)
      setDepth: 0
      setAngleY: 0
      upon: (FALL_SPEED)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (FALL_SPEED)
        upon: (TOUCH_GROUND)
          gotoLabelRequests: s32'landing'
          warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(150000), Val(0), Val(5)
          upon: (IDLING)
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(5)
              clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
              haltMomentum: 1
              setPositionXInBattle: 150000
            endIf: 
          endUpon: 
        endUpon: 
      endUpon: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Slave_Down_3_21000'
  gotoLabelRequests: s32'loop'
  createObject: s32'cmnWSB_Camera_Down_3_L', (PLAYER)
  resetMotionBlurAmount: 
  haltMomentum: 1
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(90)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(PosY), Val(10), Mem(ActReg1)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(43680000)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(87360000)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Val(1500000)
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(0)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(-1)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg2)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg2)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg3)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg3)
  endIf: 
  warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Mem(ActReg4), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg0)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(SpeedY), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActReg5)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(-1), Mem(ActReg6)
  modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ActReg0)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(ActReg5), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(Gravity)
  modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(Gravity), Val(2)
  upon: (FALL_SPEED)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (FALL_SPEED)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActionTime), Mem(ActReg6)
    pushVelocityY: 
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Val(-1)
    warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Mem(ActReg4), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg6)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Val(-1)
    popVelocityY: 
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg6), Val(-1), Mem(ActReg7)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ActReg7)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(PosY), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(Gravity)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(Gravity), Val(2)
    upon: (IDLING)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(80)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActionTime), Mem(ActReg6)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Mem(ActReg6), Val(-1), Mem(ActReg7)
        modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(ActReg7)
        modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(PosY), Mem(ActReg6), Mem(Gravity)
        modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(Gravity), Val(2)
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
    landingHeight: 0
    upon: (TOUCH_GROUND)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'landing'
      haltMomentum: 1
      warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(-700000), Val(0), Val(15)
      setAngleY: 0
      effectForDownLv2: (BACK_2_BODY), 1, 0
      effectForDownLv3: (BACK_2_BODY), 1, 0
      cameraShake: s32'ShakeTateYoko', 500, 0, 10, 5
      sendSignalName: 22, s32'WSB_Down', 0
      cmnSfx: s32'SE_BTL_CMN_Down_Def_Stone_M'
      voiceLine: s16'vxxx109'
      upon: (IDLING)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(10)
          createArgDirection: 1
          createParticleWithArg: s32'bg_dashstart', (BACK_1_BODY)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(15)
          if: Mem(HitPoint)
            if: Mem(CmnCharaReg7)
              warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(-750000), Val(0), Val(5)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'brake'
            endIf: 
            else: 
              warp: (SELF), (WORLD_ZERO), Val(-775000), Val(0), Val(5)
              jumpToStateKeepDamage: s32'CmnActKorogari'
            endElse: 
          endIf: 
          else: 
            jumpToStateKeepDamage: s32'CmnActKorogari'
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(20)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
          setPositionXInBattle: -750000
          haltMomentum: 1
          createArgDirection: 1
          createParticleWithArg: s32'bg_dashbrake', (PLAYER)
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  setDepthSpeed: 0, 777222
  upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(PosZ), Val(-777222)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
      setDepthSpeed: 0, 0
      setDepth: 0
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine:
