beginSubroutine: s32'cmn_wallbreak_eff'
  ignoreSuperFreeze: 1
  ignoreFinishStop: 1
  deactivateObjectByNameAll: s32'cmn_wallbreak_lv1'
  deactivateObjectByNameAll: s32'cmn_wallbreak_lv2'
  deactivateObjectByNameAll: s32'cmn_wallbreak_lv3'
  setObjectSize: 1250
  checkMoveFlag: (CLOSE_TO_RIGHT_CORNER)
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    faceLeft: 
  endIf: 
  checkMoveFlag: (CLOSE_TO_LEFT_CORNER)
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    faceRight: 
  endIf: 
  ifNot: Mem(SentToObject0)
    addPositionX: 0, -150000
    addPositionY: 0, 75000
    addDepth: 0, -150000
    setAngleY: -15000
  endIf: 
  else: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageSplitCount), Val(6)
      addPositionX: 0, 150000
      addPositionY: 0, 75000
      addDepth: 0, -50000
      setAngleY: -30000
    endIf: 
    else: 
      addPositionX: 0, 125000
      addPositionY: 0, 75000
      addDepth: 0, 75000
      setAngleY: 30000
    endElse: 
  endElse: 
  if: Mem(SentToObject1)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(StageSplitCount), Val(6)
      setAngleY: -10000
    endIf: 
    else: 
      setAngleY: 50000
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginState: s32'cmn_wallbreak_lv1'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_wallbreak_eff'
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'null', 1
  sprite: s32'null', 60
  linkParticle: s32'cmn_wallbreak_lv1'
endState: 

beginState: s32'cmn_wallbreak_lv2'

endState: 

beginState: s32'cmn_wallbreak_lv3'

  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_wallbreak_eff'
    cmnSfx: s32'SE_BTL_CMN_Wall_BoxJump'
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SentToObject0), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SentToObject0), Val(2)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SentToObject0), Val(3)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SentToObject0), Val(4)
    endIf: 
  endUpon:

beginSubroutine: s32'cmnZokuseiDmgCheckFunc'
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(0)
  ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(FuncArg0)
    ifOperationInObject: (IS_GREATER), (PLAYER), Mem(DamageEffectCount), Val(0)
      ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerDamage)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
    deactivateCurrentObject: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(Tmp), Val(150000)
      attackHitPositionType: (EX_POINT_3), 1, 0

  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginState: s32'cmn_kakusei_finish'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
      deactivateObjectById: (SELF)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      ignoreFinishStop: 1
      ignoreSuperFreeze: 1
      callSubroutine: s32'cmnGlareDelete'
      fadeOutStart: 0, 0
      linkObjectDirection: 2
      linkObjectSize: 2
      linkObjPosition: 2
      upon: (PRE_DRAW)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (PRE_DRAW)
        createArgTransPriority: -100
        linkParticleWithArg2: s32'cmn_kakusei_finish_total'
        storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(Angle), (PARENT), Mem(Angle)
        storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(AngleY), (PARENT), Mem(AngleY)
        storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(AngleX), (PARENT), Mem(AngleX)

  endLabel:

endState: 

beginState: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Screen_Effect'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    hideUI: 1
    cinesco: 1
    ignoreSuperFreezeFromAlly: 1
    ignoreFinishStop: 1
    ignoreZLine: 1
    cameraShake: s32'ShakeTate', 1500, 5, 25, 0
    runOnObject: (WINNER)
      slowMoveRate: 0, 3000
    endRunOnObject: 
    runOnObject: (LOSER)
      slowMoveRate: 0, 3000
    endRunOnObject: 
    storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ActReg1), (ENEMY), Mem(PosY)
    storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ActReg2), (ENEMY), Mem(SpeedY)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(-1)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(2), Mem(ActReg3)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg2)
      runOnObject: (ENEMY)
        slowMoveRate: 0, 1000
      endRunOnObject: 
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg3)
        runOnObject: (ENEMY)
          slowMoveRate: 0, 2000
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperationInObject: (IS_LESSER), (ENEMY), Mem(PosY), Val(50000)
        runOnObject: (ENEMY)
          slowMoveRate: 0, 500
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnCamCounterSlowSettings'
    resetSaturation: 1, 1
    setPostProcessSaturation: -1, 800, 40
    resetDiffusion: 1, 1
    setDiffusionLuminance: -1, 1400, 50
    setDiffusionThreshold: -1, 0, 50
    resetDOF: 1, 1
    focalDistance: -1, 700, 0
    focalRegion: -1, 0, 0
    focalNearTransition: -1, 0, 0
    focalFarTransition: -1, 500, 0
    focalNearBlurSize: -1, 0, 0
    focalFarBlurSize: -1, 5, 10
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnGlareDelete'
    createGlareEffect: 1
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Mem(Tmp)
    setGlareColor: 2, 45, 0, 127, 0, 255, 0, 255, 0, 255
    setGlareScale: 2, 45, 0, 1200, 0, 1200
    ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(Dir)
      setGlareOffset: 2, 45, 0, -300000, 0, -300000
    endIf: 
    else: 
      setGlareOffset: 2, 45, 0, 300000, 0, -300000
    endElse: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'null', 120
  sprite: s32'null', 30
  resetDOF: 0, 30
  resetSaturation: 0, 30
  resetDiffusion: 0, 30
  removeGlareEffect: 2, 45
  cinesco: 0
  sprite: s32'null', 1
  hideUI: 0
endState:

beginSubroutine: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Pattern'
  ifNotInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
    if: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
      createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Screen_Effect', (PLAYER)
      cameraShakeEX: s32'Depth', 500, 0, 150, 0, s32'shake_easeout'
    endIf: 
    else: 
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Val(600000)
        stackObjectEx: (SELF), (STACK0), 14, (ATTACKER)
        isObjectActive: (STACK0)
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          ifTrueInObject: (STACK0), Mem(IsPlayer)
            setRandom: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1), Val(3)
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
              createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Near01', (PLAYER)
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(2)
              createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Far03', (PLAYER)
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(3)
              createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Far04', (PLAYER)
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
          else: 
            createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Projectile', (PLAYER)
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
        else: 
          createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Projectile', (PLAYER)
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      else: 
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyDiffY), Val(120000)
          createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Up', (PLAYER)
        endIf: 
        else: 
          ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyDiffY), Val(-40000)
            createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Down', (PLAYER)
          endIf: 
          else: 
            ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Val(300000)
              setRandom: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1), Val(3)
              createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Zoom', (PLAYER)
              ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
              endIf: 
              ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(2)
                createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Near02', (PLAYER)
              endIf: 
              ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(3)
                createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Near03', (PLAYER)
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
            else: 
              setRandom: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1), Val(3)
              ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
                createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Near01', (PLAYER)
              endIf: 
              ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(2)
                createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Near02', (PLAYER)
              endIf: 
              ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(3)
                createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Near03', (PLAYER)
              endIf: 
            endElse: 
          endElse: 
        endElse: 
      endElse: 
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
  createObject: s32'cmnCam_FinishTimeOut', (PLAYER)
  deactivateObjectById: (SELF)
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Init'
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(0)
    fadeOutStart: 300, 1
    runOnObject: (PLAYER)
      ignoreZLine: 1
      fadeInStart: 0
    endRunOnObject: 
    runOnObject: (ENEMY)
      ignoreZLine: 1
      fadeInStart: 0
    endRunOnObject: 
    runOnObject: (WINNER)
      slowMoveRate: 0, 3000
    endRunOnObject: 
    runOnObject: (LOSER)
      slowMoveRate: 0, 3000
    endRunOnObject: 
    storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ActReg1), (ENEMY), Mem(PosY)
    storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ActReg2), (ENEMY), Mem(SpeedY)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(-1)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(2), Mem(ActReg3)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg2)
      runOnObject: (ENEMY)
        slowMoveRate: 0, 1000
      endRunOnObject: 
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg3)
        runOnObject: (ENEMY)
          slowMoveRate: 0, 2000
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperationInObject: (IS_LESSER), (ENEMY), Mem(PosY), Val(50000)
        runOnObject: (ENEMY)
          slowMoveRate: 0, 500
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnCamCounterSlowSettings'
    resetSaturation: 1, 1
    setPostProcessSaturation: -1, 800, 40
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnGlareDelete'
    createGlareEffect: 1
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Mem(Tmp)
    setGlareColor: 2, 45, 0, 127, 0, 255, 0, 255, 0, 255
    setGlareScale: 2, 45, 0, 1200, 0, 1200
    ifTrueInObject: (WINNER), Mem(Dir)
      setGlareOffset: 2, 45, 0, -300000, 0, -300000
    endIf: 
    else: 
      setGlareOffset: 2, 45, 0, 300000, 0, -300000
    endElse: 
    upon: (BEFORE_EXIT)
      resetSaturation: 0, 20
      resetDOF: 0, 40
      removeGlareEffect: 2, 45
    endUpon: 
    cinesco: 1
    hideUI: 1
    ignoreFinishStop: 1
    ignoreSuperFreeze: 1
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(0)
    ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
      deactivateObjectById: (SELF)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
        linkObjectDirection: 2
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(1)
          createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Near01', (PLAYER)
          addPositionY: 0, 600000
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(2)
          createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Near02', (PLAYER)
          addPositionY: 0, 400000
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(3)
          createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Near03', (PLAYER)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(4)
          createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Far04', (PLAYER)
          addPositionY: 0, 300000
          setAngleY: -75000
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(5)
          createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Zoom', (PLAYER)
          addPositionY: 0, 300000
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(6)
          createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Tilt', (PLAYER)
          addPositionY: 0, 400000
          setAngleY: 40000
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(7)
          createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Projectile', (PLAYER)
          addPositionY: 0, 0
          setAngleY: 70000
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(8)
          createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Up', (PLAYER)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(9)
          createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Down', (PLAYER)
          setAngleX: -30000
          setAngleY: 60000
        endIf: 
        createObjectWithArg: s32'cmn_kakusei_finish', (PLAYER)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Screen_Effect', (PLAYER)
        cameraShakeEX: s32'Depth', 2000, 0, 150, 0, s32'shake_easeout'
      endElse: 
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginState: s32'cmnWorldStop_Obj'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    deactivateObjectByNameExceptSelf: s32'cmnWorldStop_Obj'
    upon: (AFTER_FRAME_STEP_EX)
      ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (AFTER_FRAME_STEP_EX)
        ifNot: Mem(SentToObject0)
          runOnObject: (PLAYER)
            callSubroutine: s32'cmnWorldStop_End'
          endRunOnObject: 
        endIf: 
        else: 
          runOnObject: (PLAYER)
            callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmnWorldStop_End', Val(1), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
          endRunOnObject: 
        endElse: 
        deactivateCurrentObject: 
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
    upon: (AFTER_EXIT)
      debugLogForScript: s32'ON_PLAYER_ACTION_CHANGE', 0, 0
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (AFTER_EXIT)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (AFTER_FRAME_STEP_EX)
      deactivateCurrentObject: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'null', 2147483647
endState:
